###Post-War###
shared_focus = {
	id = MTS_southeastern_triumph
	x = 8
	y = 0
	
	cost = 1
	allow_branch = {
		MTS_has_scorched_as_leader = yes
		has_country_flag = MTS_conquered_southeast
		OR = {
			SLW = {
				exists = yes
				has_completed_focus = SLW_everypony_to_daybreaker
			}
			EQS = {
